Sherrie Kapssof<//name>
<Time>1446327183133</Time><Rate>1<//Rate>< Text>
I'm not one to go out of my way to write up complaints unless needed, but this calls for it.

1) Cost
From day 1, the manager, Jim, told us they are 30% cheaper than the dealership price with a free evaluation. We were very pleased with the things he had to say on the phone, so we decided to go ahead and have them work on my car. After they diagnosed it, found out it was an $800 charge, whereas Ford's price was $125. The price we got from Ford was about $4,000 for a new transmission including labor and all. Jim told us it would be between $1500-$2500. Later in the week, he changed his answer to $3800 for the final price. I couldn't take it to Ford where I would've rather taken it back to because I was apparently down $800 regardless, so we stayed with not much of a choice.

2) Rental/charge
The first thing he told us was the rentals were free. Another time, told us only the $25 rental was free (a Fiat). We had the "upgraded" car that was $40 so he said he'd take off $25 off each day. Great! When I was picking up my car, I found out he had tacked on all the charges on top of the original price he gave us. The whole cost of this entire thing was about $4500. The "discounted" price should have been off the $3800 total that he gave us. He failed to provide us with those details. Not only was that inching toward one grand more than his original price, his quote of "30% cheaper than the dealership price" was invalid.

3) Timeframe/duration
Day one, he told us it would be 3-5 days until I have my car back. We had it towed over there on Tuesday and told us they would call us Friday and again, changed his answer to 5-7 days. That following Monday, he calls and tells us that they barely took it apart and gave us the cost. He then told us it should be ready Wednesday. Wednesday comes and they test drove it and it jolted when changing gears so they had to work on it and would be ready Thursday. Thursday comes, nothing. Finally got my car back today (Saturday) with no communication in between.

Overall, we will not be doing business with them again. We don't work with shady liars and will be contacting the headquarters about all of this. The lack of communication is very unprofessional. The fact that he tacked on money we weren't aware of is very unprofessional. We were taken advantage of and it ruined the entire company for us. I hope you're proud, Jim.<//Text>

<Text>I'm not one to go out of my way to write up complaints unless needed, but this calls for it.

1) Cost
From day 1, the manager, Jim, told us they are 30% cheaper than the dealership price with a free evaluation. We were very pleased with the things he had to say on the phone, so we decided to go ahead and have them work on my car. After they diagnosed it, found out it was an $800 charge, whereas Ford's price was $125. The price we got from Ford was about $4,000 for a new transmission including labor and all. Jim told us it would be between $1500-$2500. Later in the week, he changed his answer to $3800 for the final price. I couldn't take it to Ford where I would've rather taken it back to because I was apparently down $800 regardless, so we stayed with not much of a choice.

2) Rental/charge
The first thing he told us was the rentals were free. Another time, told us only the $25 rental was free (a Fiat). We had the "upgraded" car that was $40 so he said he'd take off $25 off each day. Great! When I was picking up my car, I found out he had tacked on all the charges on top of the original price he gave us. The whole cost of this entire thing was about $4500. The "discounted" price should have been off the $3800 total that he gave us. He failed to provide us with those details. Not only was that inching toward one grand more than his original price, his quote of "30% cheaper than the dealership price" was invalid.

3) Timeframe/duration
Day one, he told us it would be 3-5 days until I have my car back. We had it towed over there on Tuesday and told us they would call us Friday and again, changed his answer to 5-7 days. That following Monday, he calls and tells us that they barely took it apart and gave us the cost. He then told us it should be ready Wednesday. Wednesday comes and they test drove it and it jolted when changing gears so they had to work on it and would be ready Thursday. Thursday comes, nothing. < review>
My daughter and I thought the birria was delicious! Very authentic.

I must have literally driven past this restaurant without noticing it hundreds of times over the years. It is very easy to miss; small, no flashy sign, and just blends into the little strip of business where it is located. It is not a fancy, but we were treated very well by the family who owns and operates this business. The service and food were both great, and I will definitely be going back again!< /review>

<date>1542667094540< /date><user_id>111574532729357790876</user_id><gmapID>0x80855956fedf6e31:0xe881480205586b2f</gmapID><rating>4</rating><Pictures>[{'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNeLFK2ns7LQJXFIOdFaZUSswh8kOtvg-Ja5ABK=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOeAD7a9_WinZjMzKJ_wo2H-wwvvMvklGc2Ol72=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipNeQlTc6JNHCJAISfFtJ2KpA-JgEsK08PDsQIit=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipOJY_TW_8fzAGccIU4L_ATuHhLIvcVFoOlZJnca=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipMRqJWB846MSDfCEQ2hYM6nxp70FIDRmy0tjDKZ=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipM_6bE6WdD4LLM97H0GU-SEg52-dXpxOIAPLr8R=w150-h150-k-no-p']}, {'url': ['https://lh5.googleusercontent.com/p/AF1QipO3yQblwOER7McqdDOTpXeU_zCdk0PKFDplEZou=w150-h150-k-no-p']}]< /Pictures><resp>None</resp><review>Mexican spot tucked at the end of a small strip mall sharing the parking lot with a sports bar and liquor store. I was the only one who wasn't speaking Spanish while I was there.

As their name implies, birria is their specialty with Birria de Res (beef) and Birria de Chivo (goat) available in both seca (dry) and caldo (soup) forms. Menudo and pozole also are listed under Specialties  and other Mexican standards are on the menu like burritos, tacos, enchiladas, and tortas.

The Caldo version comes with corn tortillas, lemon and lime wedges, and topped with onions, cilantro and salsa. The broth is flavorful and mildly spicy. The goat meat was tender and not too gamey.

I liked it, but thought it was a little pricey at just under $13.

Friendly service.<//review></record>

< text>
Arguably the best dining hall on campus. Doesn't necessarily mean the food is spectacular, but you get your money's worth and if you have to choose a dining hall on campus, this is usually the best bet. Good array of food. You can count on there always being pizza, cereal, soup, and a salad bar. Also always an option of fruit and pastry. The rest of the menu switches out. Seating can be hard to find but is usually okay, especially when they open up the MPR for additional seating. Is open the longest and most often out of all the dining halls on campus.< /text>

Just to let you know, I have a terrible phobia of dentists. I finally got the courage to proceed with dental surgery. In August,  I had a tooth extracted and two implants in one visit. <text>The pioneer is an iconic watering hole for bikers and billionaires. It's been operating since the late 19th century. It's main attraction is the music program which has some of the greatest talent both local and national, featured on the small Dusty stage. This is a very casual place, often a destination by those on horse back-who park out back.  Weeknights, you might walk in and find a #1 artist playing the guitar to 5 people in the bar. On weekends, when big headliners like Dutch Uncle play, expect to mingle in a very packed bar with captains of industry from the local area, and the regular folk who are all there to party and enjoy life. Even for people who rarely get out, this is not a place to miss.< /text>< pictures>
